/* Allfusion Harvest Default Database Schema */


WHENEVER SQLERROR EXIT FAILURE
spool &1

define HARVESTMETA   = &2
define HARVESTBLOB   = &3
define HARVESTINDEX  = &4

set heading off
set feedback on
set timing off
set verify off
set serveroutput on
set document on

/* TABLES */

CREATE TABLE "HARVERSIONDATA" (
	"VERSIONDATAOBJID" NUMBER NOT NULL, 
	"REFCOUNTER" NUMBER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL, 
	"DATASIZE" NUMBER NOT NULL, 
	"COMPRESSED" CHAR(1) NOT NULL, 
	"COMPDATASIZE" NUMBER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL, 
	"FILEACCESS" CHAR(9), 
	"MODIFYTIME" DATE, 
	"CREATETIME" DATE, 
	"DCB" VARCHAR2(256), 
	"TEXTFILE" NUMBER NOT NULL, 
	"ITEMOBJID" NUMBER DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL, 
	"VERSIONDATA" BLOB)  
	   PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 LOGGING 
	   STORAGE(INITIAL 10240 NEXT 10240 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645 PCTINCREASE 0 
	           FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT) 
	TABLESPACE "&HARVESTBLOB" LOB ("VERSIONDATA") 
	   STORE AS ( ENABLE STORAGE IN ROW TABLESPACE "&HARVESTBLOB" CHUNK 2048 PCTVERSION 0 NOCACHE NOLOGGING 
	           STORAGE (INITIAL 26263552 NEXT 26214400 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 999 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 
	                    FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT) 
	           INDEX "HARDATA_LOBINDEX" (TABLESPACE "&HARVESTBLOB" INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 
	           STORAGE (INITIAL 5242880 NEXT 5242880 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 999 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 
	                    BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT)));


CREATE TABLE "HARVERSIONDELTA" (
	"CHILDVERSIONDATAID" NUMBER NOT NULL, 
	"PARENTVERSIONDATAID" NUMBER NOT NULL, 
	"DELTASIZE" NUMBER NOT NULL, 
	"VERSIONDELTA" BLOB)  
	PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 LOGGING 
	STORAGE(INITIAL 10240 NEXT 10240 MINEXTENTS 1 
	MAXEXTENTS 2147483645 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT) 
	TABLESPACE "&HARVESTBLOB" LOB ("VERSIONDELTA") 
	STORE AS ( ENABLE STORAGE IN ROW TABLESPACE "&HARVESTBLOB" CHUNK 2048 PCTVERSION 0 NOCACHE NOLOGGING 
	STORAGE (INITIAL 59392 NEXT 10240 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 
	BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT) INDEX (TABLESPACE "&HARVESTBLOB" INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 
	STORAGE (INITIAL 10240 NEXT 10240 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 
	         BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT)));

/* PR4943, e.USD Integration */
 

CREATE VIEW "HARAPPROVEHISTVIEW" 
	("ENVOBJID"
	,"STATEOBJID"
	,"PACKAGEOBJID"
	,"USROBJID"
	,"ACTIONTIME") AS SELECT UNIQUE
	envobjid
	, stateobjid
	, packageobjid
	, usrobjid
	, MAX(execdtime)
FROM   harApproveHist
GROUP BY envobjid
	, stateobjid
	, packageobjid
	, usrobjid;


CREATE VIEW "HARAPPROVEHISTACTIONVIEW" 
	("ENVOBJID"
	,"STATEOBJID"
	,"PACKAGEOBJID"
	,"USROBJID"
	,"ACTIONTIME"
	,"ACTION"
	,"NOTE") AS SELECT h.envobjid
	,h.stateobjid
	,h.packageobjid
	,h.usrobjid
	,h.execdtime
	,h.action
	,h.note
     FROM harApproveHist h
	, harApproveHistView v
	, harpackage p
    WHERE v.packageobjid = p.packageobjid
      AND v.stateobjid = p.stateobjid
      AND h.envobjid = v.envobjid
      AND h.stateobjid = v.stateobjid
      AND h.packageobjid = v.packageobjid
      AND h.usrobjid = v.usrobjid
      AND h.execdtime = v.actiontime;


CREATE VIEW "HARAPPROVEACTIONVIEW" 
	("ENVOBJID"
	,"STATEOBJID"
	,"PACKAGEOBJID"
	,"USROBJID"
	,"ACTIONTIME"
	,"ACTION"
	,"USRGRPOBJID"
	,"PROCESSOBJID") AS
       SELECT 
	v.envobjid,
	v.stateobjid,
      	v.packageobjid,
       	v.usrobjid,
       	v.actiontime,
       	v.action,
       	l.usrgrpobjid,
       	l.processobjid
     	FROM harApproveHistActionView v , harApproveList l
    	WHERE v.stateobjid = l.stateobjid
      	AND (  (   l.isgroup = 'N'
             AND l.usrobjid = v.usrobjid)
          OR (   l.isgroup = 'Y'
             AND l.usrgrpobjid IN (SELECT usrgrpobjid
                                     FROM harusersingroup g
                                    WHERE v.usrobjid = g.usrobjid)));

During check in, Allfusion Harvest compares the items in the repository to the files being checked in.  If a file does not currently exist in the repository, it will be created as a new item.  If the file already exists in the repository, the reserve tag is removed and a new version is created.  If no changes exist between the reserved version and the checked-in file, the reserve tag is simply removed.','Y','Y','Y','N','N','N')

INSERT INTO HARENVIRONMENT (
ENVOBJID, ENVIRONMENTNAME, ENVISACTIVE, BASELINEVIEWID, CREATIONTIME, CREATORID, MODIFIEDTIME, MODIFIERID, NOTE, ISARCHIVE, ARCHIVEBY, ARCHIVEMACHINE, ARCHIVEFILE, ARCHIVETIME

VALUES (
3,'Release Model','T',15,sysdate,1,sysdate,1,'The Release Model is used by organizations that make many changes to an application and release those changes as a group identified by a release number.  That
release is then taken and used as a starting point for the next development effort.
The default Release Model has three basic states: Development, Test, and
Release.  Changes are isolated in each state so that the changes made in Development wont affect the testing effort, and the contents of Test do not affect the
versions that have been released.
The flow through the life cycle starts when a fix is required and a package is created.  This package has an associated
change request form which details the changes that are needed.	Anyone can create a change package.  When the change is ready for work, the software is checked
out for update and the changes are made.  The changes are then checked back into Allfusion Harvest and are associated with the initiating package.  When the changes
are ready for implementation, the packages are promoted to the Test state.  When all the testing is done, the packages are promoted to the Release state.
When
the next release is ready to begin, or if an emergency fix needs to implemented, a snapshot is created.  This snapshot is used to create a new project where
additional development will be isolated.  For example, you are working on Release 1.0 and it is out for Beta testing.  You now want to start working on Release
2.0.  You would create a snapshot of Release 1.0 Beta and use it to create the Release 2.0 project.  Any changes made to the Release 2.0 project will
not be seen by the Release 1.0 project, and visa versa.','N',1,'','','')
;

6,'Parallel Development Model','T',31,sysdate,1,sysdate,1,'This life cycle is intended to be used to control the flow of changes in a development effort. Packages are moved from the problem project or created in the
Assigned Changes state. Then they are promoted to Coding so changes may begin. They continue through Unit Testing, Quality Assurance, and finally Closed.  This
model supports parallel development by allowing developers to checkout for concurrent update and forcing them to always merge their changes from the branches

INSERT INTO HARENVIRONMENT (
ENVOBJID, ENVIRONMENTNAME, ENVISACTIVE, BASELINEVIEWID, CREATIONTIME, CREATORID, MODIFIEDTIME, MODIFIERID, NOTE, ISARCHIVE, ARCHIVEBY, ARCHIVEMACHINE, ARCHIVEFILE, ARCHIVETIME
)
VALUES (
7,'Production Model','T',36,sysdate,1,sysdate,1,'The Production Model is used by organizations that have an operational project that must be kept running and which has constant changes that need to be
added.	There is no concept of a release.  Changes are added as needed.
The default Production Model has five basic states: Development, Merge, Test, Staging
and Production.  It also includes an Emergency state.  The Development, Emergency and Production states are in the Production view, guaranteeing that any
changes made to the software will be based on the versions in production. 
The flow through the life cycle starts when a fix is needed to production.  A
package is created that will track the work through the life cycle, and a change request form that describes the required changes is associated with the
package.  Anyone can create a change package.  When the change is ready for work, items are checked out for Concurrent Update, which places the changes on a
branch.  After the change is made, it is checked back into that branch and is associated with the initiating package.  When the changes are ready for
implementation, packages are promoted to the Merge state, which belongs to the Merge view.
Once the changes are merged to the trunk, the packages are promoted
to the Test state in the Test view.  This allows testers to test out the changes without affecting the Production view, and isolates the changes so that updates
in the Merge view do not affect the Test view.	When all the testing is done, the packages are promoted to the Staging state, which allows the Production
manager to pull those changes into the production project.	During this promotion, if an item in the packages being promoted also has a version associated
with a package in the Emergency Package Group, the package promotion will fail. When the packages are promoted from Staging to Production, the changes become
visible in the Production view and are ready for the next round of changes.','N',1,'','','')
;

added.	There is no concept of a release.  Changes are added as needed.
The default Production Model has five basic states: Development, Merge, Test, Staging
and Production.  It also includes an Emergency state.  The Development, Emergency and Production states are in the Production view, guaranteeing that any
changes made to the software will be based on the versions in production.  
The flow through the life cycle starts when a fix is needed to production.  A
package is created that will track the work through the life cycle, and a change request form that describes the required changes is associated with the
package.  Anyone can create a change package.  When the change is ready for work, items are checked out for Concurrent Update, which places the changes on a
branch.  After the change is made, it is checked back into that branch and is associated with the initiating package.  When the changes are ready for
implementation, packages are promoted to the Merge state, which belongs to the Merge view.
Once the changes are merged to the trunk, the packages are promoted
to the Test state in the Test view.  This allows testers to test out the changes without affecting the Production view, and isolates the changes so that updates
in the Merge view do not affect the Test view.	When all the testing is done, the packages are promoted to the Staging state, which allows the Production
manager to pull those changes into the production project.	During this promotion, if an item in the packages being promoted also has a version associated
with a package in the Emergency Package Group, the package promotion will fail. When the packages are promoted from Staging to Production, the changes become
visible in the Production view and are ready for the next round of changes.
When an Emergency fix is needed, a package is crea',181,355,0
)

	ON "HARALLCHILDRENPATH" ("CHILDITEMID" )   
	TABLESPACE "&HARVESTINDEX";

	ON "HARALLCHILDRENPATH" ("ITEMOBJID" , "CHILDITEMID" )         
	TABLESPACE "&HARVESTINDEX";

	ADD CONSTRAINT "HARALLCHILDRENPATH_PK" PRIMARY KEY 
	("ITEMOBJID"
	, "CHILDITEMID") USING INDEX        
	TABLESPACE "&HARVESTINDEX";

   REFERENCES HARPACKAGE (PACKAGEOBJID) ON DELETE CASCADE;

   REFERENCES HARFORM (FORMOBJID) ON DELETE CASCADE;

   REFERENCES HARFORMATTACHMENT (ATTACHMENTOBJID) ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE harPackage ADD notifywebservice CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL;
